style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而吞馒头吞饭这样的动作，则可能将鱼刺越带越深，刺破食管或刺破血管，风险更大。</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">实在取不出来就别勉强，赶紧去医院，让专业的耳鼻喉医生或内镜医生来处理吧。</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p A 含量也高于普通牛奶。</p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">维生素 A</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 50%;border-style: none;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);border-style: none;border-width: 1px;padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgba(240, 214, 19, 0) 0px 0px 0px;border-radius: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: -5px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">69 微克</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 50%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);border-style: none;border-width: 1px;padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgba(240, 214, 19, 0) 0px 0px 0px;border-radius: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: -5px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">46 微克</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin: 0px 0% 5px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px 5px;font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"text-align: center;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">营养越多，不一定越好</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(161, 142, 214, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">你可能会觉得：既然水牛奶营养更高，当然应该推荐大家都来喝啊。但其实食品和营养学的专业人士的建议是：</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">对一种食品进行综合评价的时候，不能只看单项的营养含量高不高，还要看能达到补足营养的性价比。有些时候，高营养也意味着营养过剩的可能。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">虽然水牛奶在营养含量方面高于普通牛奶，但是有些营养也不是越多越好——水牛奶中的脂肪含量高达 7.5% 以上，是普通牛奶的 2~3 倍。水牛奶中的反式脂肪酸占总脂肪酸的比例（3.61%），也略高于普通牛奶（2.79%）。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.54\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1000\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/Pvr3FasqXd5cCPYKR56xfkvd3iaS4G0GctypIQGNKjIyclWKldicM9JxSExoKRUc0phhS4icMNPYrbFsE3l8AE1nA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);padding: 10px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 5px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;padding: 0px 5px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">心血管疾病专家推荐每日饱和脂肪酸摄入不要超过脂肪总量的三分之一（约 20 克）。</p></section></section><section style=\"margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: right;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(206, 206, 206);padding: 0px 5px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"text-align: center;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">图片来源：站酷海洛</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">其实，如果想补充更高的蛋白质和钙的话，多喝一点普通牛奶就能打平了。但如果买水牛奶，往往价格贵至少一倍，还有可能脂肪摄入过量，值得吗？</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin: 0px 0% 5px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px 5px;font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"text-align: center;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">去掉脂肪，口感就要打折扣</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(161, 142, 214, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">很多人买水牛奶都是被「像冰淇淋一样的口感」这句宣传语打动。的确有很多网友表示：太好喝了！喝过水牛奶以后，发现以前喝的奶都太寡淡了。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">前面说过，水牛奶的蛋白质含量和脂肪含量都更好，而这两点也是决定牛奶口感的重要因素。这种特点让水牛奶的价值在制作奶类食品时得到了最大发挥，比如双皮奶、黄油、奶酪，如果用水牛奶做原料，都会更容易得到更好的品质。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.545\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1000\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/Pvr3FasqXd5cCPYKR56xfkvd3iaS4G0GcuvMVpVROfZ1PDnu3NXH5dot2fyMqPlsgOlrHVqJnd9Sn2WGcx0FO4g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);padding: 10px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 5px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;padding: 0px 5px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">你可能在吃披萨或者吃希腊沙拉时，会注意到点缀其间的「小白球」，它就是水牛奶做成的奶酪。</p></section></section><section style=\"margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: right;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(206, 206, 206);padding: 0px 5px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">但是，大部分消费者是买回家天天喝的，高脂肪这一点还是很令人担忧，所以市面上卖得比较火的几款水牛奶，其实都是「部分脱脂」。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">不光包装上写得明明白白，看成分表也会发现：脂肪含量比起上文研究中的数据要少了近一半。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.1995163\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"827\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/Pvr3FasqXd5cCPYKR56xfkvd3iaS4G0GcBiaUtegVgPwVGHazSVTBQfHJrpcH3mdkmY4dsMdH3La3a5iaQuydMEMQ/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin: 15px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(206, 206, 206);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.6px;padding: 0px 10px;box-sizing: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">那，被夸上天的「浓郁口感」真的有那么明显吗？</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">研究所观察了一下销量比较高的几款水牛奶的买家评论区，有人赞不绝口，也有人觉得失望。随机采访了几位消费者，有人表示，喝起来有点像少糖版的旺*牛奶，略带甜味儿反而让他觉得没那么习惯了。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">坦白说，口感这么主观的事，我们还是建议你自己去试试。好喝和低脂如何两全，向来都是个难题。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin: 0px 0% 5px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px 5px;font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"text-align: center;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">价格高，还可能买到假货</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(161, 142, 214, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">水牛奶没有成为市场上的主流，是因为水牛奶的产量远远不如牛奶，大约只占了全球牛奶产量的12%。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">有限的产量以及人们对水牛奶与日俱增的需求也让水牛奶的价格居高不下：纯水牛奶的价格经常是普通纯牛奶的至少 2 倍，比起高端的纯牛奶价格也高出了不少。</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(0, 0, normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">研究发现，99.7% 的宫颈癌与 HPV（人乳头瘤病毒）感染有关。正因如此，HPV 疫苗作为目前全世界唯一一个可以有效预防癌症的疫苗一直以来被高度关注，甚至一针难求。</p><p 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 感染主要是通过性生活感染，有不洁性生活者（高危性接触，例如多个性伴侣）的确有更高的感染风险。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">但这并不意味着感染 HPV，就一定有不良的性生活。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">现实生活中，HPV 病毒非常常见，即使常规的性生活也有感染风险。HPV 感染通常会在 12 个月内缓解（1～2 年内检测可由阳转阴）。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而且，性生活并不是 HPV 感染的唯一途径。HPV 也可以通过间接方式感染，例如接触感染者的衣物、洗漱用品等。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">有数据显示，至少 80% 的性行为活跃者在一生中会暴露于 HPV 一次，有些人甚至不知道自己感染过。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0;\"><br></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"justify-content: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">对于大部分人而言，只是一过性的感染病毒而已，还不至于对身体造成伤害，</strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif>只有极少数的 HPV 感染会最终发展成疾病。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif><br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: sans-serif>目前发现，只有持续性感染高危 HPV 亚型，才有机会出现宫颈癌前病变。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif></span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif>通常，医院在检测到高危 HPV 感染时会要求做进一步的检查。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果宫颈 TCT 检查正常，阴道镜活检也排除了宫颈病变的情况下，是不需要做任何手术的，更不需要切除子宫。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: style=\"background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;padding-bottom: 30px;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">目前没有发现有任何药物可以有效的治疗 HPV 感染。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">医学上，只能对病毒引起的病变进行治疗，但如果只是检测到感染（阳性），并不需要治疗。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">赶跑 HPV 病毒的最好的方法就是增强免疫力，同时尽量避免反复感染的诱发因素。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">一方面可以通过保证充足的睡眠、合理的作息、适当的运动、减少压力、避免吸烟等来改善；<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">另一方面就是要避免诱因，例如同房要用避孕套、避免不洁性生活、避免阴道炎的发生等。</span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 感染不止女性会有，男性也会感染 HPV。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 可以感染阴茎和睾丸等部位。有研究发现，伴侣感染同类型 HPV 类型发生率接近 25%。而男性同样会向女性传播 HPV。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">避孕套虽然能降低 HPV 感染风险，但不能做到 100% 的阻断 HPV，在避孕套没有覆盖的部位仍然有可能感染 HPV。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在双方都感染的情况下，同房会带来的反复交叉感染，影响女性 HPV 转阴，同时增加宫颈病变的风险。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如果女性发现有反复感染的情况，也建议另一半去做相关检查。</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: border-box;\">误区：打 HPV 疫苗增加宫颈癌风险</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;padding-bottom: 30px;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 疫苗是预防宫颈癌的。它通过重组基因表达 L1 蛋白合成病毒样颗粒，它采用的并不是活疫苗，也不含有HPV DNA，疫苗本身不会对人体带来危害。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">病毒样颗粒能最终保护人体的机制是：通过模拟病毒的样子，刺激人体免疫系统认识病毒并产生保护性抗体，这种抗体会存在于人的体液中。当真正的 病毒入侵人体，抗体会立即作用，将其清除，阻止 HPV 致病。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">本质上， HPV 疫苗作用原理其实和乙肝病毒疫苗等病毒疫苗类似，就像乙肝疫苗不会增加肝癌风险一样，HPV 疫苗也不会增加宫颈癌风险，都是安全的。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"margin: 40px 0% 30px;text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);flex: 0 0 auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 22px;height: 22px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: -40px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 36px;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: -0.5px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">06 </strong></em></p></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;height: auto;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">误区：有了性生活，打疫苗就没用了</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;padding-bottom: 30px;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV （人乳头瘤病毒）是一个大家族，包含 200 多个亚型，主要通过性行为传播，性生活确实会增加感染风险。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 疫苗是通过提前对某几类高风险的 HPV 亚型产生抵抗，从而预防疾病。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">有性生活的人，可能已经感染了几种 HPV，接种疫苗的获益的确变小了。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">但这并不意味着有性生活后疫苗就没用了，性生活通常不会让人感染到疫苗所覆盖的所有 HPV 亚型，对没有感染的 HPV 亚型，接种疫苗仍然有预防作用。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;padding-top: 3px;padding-bottom: 6px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid none;border-color: rgb(239, 241, 236) rgb(219, 219, 219);width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;margin: -20px 0% -5px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 35px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_svg/uI5pczeERTaojrtwdASJEAMvhR3gVbXK3xfZ9MBOic2T3QGJD89rzQscySCvgIVlw4NZEvuLYQu19MQcrBOdj1HR1ZKh66icIX/640?wx_fmt=svg\"></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">例如 4 价 HPV 疫苗，能够预防 4 个亚型的病毒：16、18、6、11。假如性生活让女性无意中感染了 6 和 11 两种 HPV 亚型，那么打 4 价疫苗对 6 和 11 型病毒的效果不佳，但它还能预防 16 和 18 两种病毒亚型。</p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: right;margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: -30px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 35px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: 价疫苗的效果是相当的，重点预防的都是高危 16 和 18 型的 HPV 亚型。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">国产疫苗最大的优势是价格，同样是 2 价疫苗，国产的价格只有进口价格的一半，也是一个很好的选择。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section border-box;\"><section style=\"justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 22px;height: 22px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: -40px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 36px;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: -0.5px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">09 </strong></em></p></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;height: auto;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">误区：过了 26 岁，没必要打疫苗</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;padding-bottom: 30px;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 疫苗之所以有对年龄的限制，一方面和疫苗临床试验的对象年龄有关，一方面也考虑了感染病毒的几率。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">一般认为，随着性生活频率的增加，感染 HPV 疫苗所覆盖的亚型的可能性会逐渐增加（接触病毒的可能性变高）。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">26 岁并不是一个绝对的年龄限制，如果在 26 岁后仍没有性生活，感染 HPV 的可能性较小，那么打疫苗能获得收益仍然很高。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">当然，随着年龄增加，接种疫苗后获得的抗体效力会不如年轻人，能早打还是更推荐的。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">而对于一般 26 岁之后的人群，目前仍有两类疫苗推荐选择：</p><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\"><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">2 价可接种人群为 9～45 岁</p></li><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">4 价可接种人群为 20～45 岁</p></li></ul></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">误区：打疫苗前，要做 HPV 检测</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;padding-bottom: 30px;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">目前国内 HPV 检测主要针对高危型，并不会覆盖所有亚型。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也就是说，即使检测出来 HPV 阳性，也只是说明感染了某种亚型，而不一定是感染所有亚型。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 疫苗对没有感染的 HPV 亚型仍然有预防作用。</span><span style=\"font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif>所以，没有必要专门为了要不要打HPV疫苗而去做检测。</span><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">换句话说，不论检测结果如何，都不影响能否接种。决定了，就去打。</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 36px;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: -0.5px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p 疫苗就不会得宫颈癌</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"background-color: rgba(0, powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"justify-content: center;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: style=\"justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p line=\"TU7B\" style=\"margin-top: 0pt;margin-bottom: 0pt;outline: none;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" pingfang sc color emoji helvetica tahoma arial sans gb yahei sans-serif start normal auto rgb><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"outline: none;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: \" microsoft yahei sans-serif>HPV 疫苗虽然能有效预防宫颈癌的发生，但它也有自己的局限性，例如</span><span style=\"outline: none;box-sizing: border-box;\">不能清除已经存在的病毒；不能改变已有的病变；不能预防所有的病毒亚型。</span></span></p><p line=\"PBDz\" style=\"margin-top: 0pt;margin-bottom: 0pt;outline: none;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" pingfang sc color emoji helvetica tahoma arial sans gb yahei sans-serif start normal auto rgb><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"> </span></p><p line=\"8kJg\" style=\"margin-top: 0pt;margin-bottom: 0pt;outline: none;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" pingfang sc color emoji helvetica tahoma arial sans gb yahei sans-serif start normal auto rgb><span style=\"outline: none;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\">因此，即使打了 HPV 疫苗，也推荐 25 岁以上，有性生活史的女性，定期做好宫颈癌筛查：</span></p><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\"><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">30 岁以下，推荐单独筛查宫颈 TCT（宫颈脱落细胞学检测），3 年检查一次；</p></li><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">30 岁以上，推荐 HPV 和宫颈 TCT 联合筛查，5 年检查一次。</p></li></ul></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">HPV 疫苗打不打，或者打哪一种，都应该根据自身的情况去选择，而当我们面对 HPV 病毒的时候，也不需要过度恐慌，做好定期复查和筛查就好。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">关于 HPV 疫苗如何选择，我们帮大家整理了一张全解析的表格，后台回复<span style=\"color: rgb(142, 116, 211);box-sizing: border-box;\">「HPV」</span>即可获得。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 18px;padding-right: 20px;padding-left: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">不同价疫苗的区别是什么？</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">漏种怎么办？</p><p style=\"box-sizing:
